### [45] [WorldKernel: A World Model is the Coupling Kernel of Admissible Possible Worlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10934)
*Fabio Rovai*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文揭示了一个反直觉的失败模式：即使在足够多的观测和干预数据下，强预测器在可识别量上表现良好，但在不可识别的反事实耦合上会崩溃至一个点（甚至可能无效），而真实值是一个数据再多也无法缩小的可容许区间。其根源是预测器无法表示跨世界耦合的不确定性。论文将世界模型建模为耦合核，其对角元对应普通后验（预测器可恢复），非对角元对应反事实耦合（预测器无法恢复），并系统研究了该非对角元的理论、边界、逻辑约束、获取机制及其重建的计算复杂性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战"足够数据+足够强预测器即可解决因果推断问题"的普遍假设，揭示预测方法在反事实推断中的根本性局限，并建立理解这种局限的理论框架。

Method: 将世界模型形式化为半正定耦合核K(T,T')，通过其对角元（普通后验）与非对角元（跨世界耦合）的区分来解释预测器的能力边界；利用半正定性作为部分识别约束以多项式时间界反事实；引入本体论公理收紧边界；设计靶向约束获取策略加速耦合重建；并将完整重建归约为可容许世界的近似计数问题。

Result: 发现预测器在28%的因果模型上会收敛到任何有效模型都无法产生的无效点；半正定性约束可在多项式时间内界反事实（而精确响应类型程序不可解）；本体论公理将边界收紧达三分之一；靶向约束获取比非靶向快数倍；耦合重建在下临界阈值下可处理、以上不可近似。

Conclusion: 预测范式内在地无法表征反事实耦合的不确定性，需要显式建模跨世界耦合结构；半正定性和逻辑约束提供了有效的计算缓解手段，但完整重建面临根本性的计算复杂性障碍。

Abstract: A common assumption holds that enough observational and interventional data, given to a strong enough predictor, suffices. We report a failure mode that contradicts it. Across hundreds of structural causal models, on identified quantities a strong predictor and a Bayesian baseline both succeed, but on unidentified quantities (the couplings between counterfactual worlds) the predictor collapses to a point, on 28% of models to one no valid model can produce, while the truth is an admissible interval more data never narrows. The gap is structural: prediction cannot represent uncertainty over counterfactual couplings. We cast a world model as a single positive semidefinite coupling kernel K(T,T') over admissible worlds, whose diagonal is the ordinary posterior (what a predictor recovers) and whose off-diagonal is the cross-world coupling it cannot, which every counterfactual reads. The paper is the theory of that off-diagonal. It is real: two states with identical posteriors differ on a cross-world query, and the off-diagonal is the coupling that fixes counterfactuals. It can be bounded: positive semidefiniteness is partial-identifying information the marginals lack, and enforcing it bounds counterfactuals in polynomial time where the exact response-type program is intractable. Logical structure sharpens it: ontology axioms tighten the bound by up to a third, propagating to couplings they never touch. It can be acquired: targeted scars, constraints learned from encountered infeasibilities, close the gap several times faster than untargeted ones. Its full reconstruction is approximate counting of the admissible worlds, tractable below the Sly-Sun threshold and inapproximable above; we do not claim to beat the worst case.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持久记忆系统旨在通过存储用户信念让LLMs更"有帮助"，但可能牺牲"正确性"——模型会系统性地放大谄媚行为，优先同意用户而非保持准确。目前缺乏对此效应的系统性评估。

Method: 构建MIST基准测试（包含科学、医学、道德推理领域用户表达合理误解的多轮合成对话），在三种最先进的记忆系统和五个模型家族上进行测试，并通过错误分析识别记忆提取为主要原因。

Abstract: Persistent memory systems promise to make LLMs more helpful by storing user beliefs over time. We show they also make models less correct by systematically amplifying sycophancy, wherein models prioritize agreement with users over accuracy. We conduct the first systematic evaluation of this effect, introducing MIST: a benchmark of synthetically generated multi-turn conversations where users express plausible misconceptions in scientific, medical, and moral reasoning domains. Testing across three state-of-the-art memory systems and five model families reveals that memory amplifies sycophantic behavior across all conditions, with up to 25x higher sycophancy rates than in-context baselines. Error analyses suggest memory extraction as the primary culprit: lossy compression into discrete snippets encodes user misconceptions while discarding corrective context. Based on these results, we propose two lightweight mitigations that substantially reduce sycophancy while matching or exceeding memory systems at factual recall.

The generated DSL can be rasterized into semantic masks and used to condition a Flux-based LoRA renderer, producing realistic blueprint-style furnished floor-plan images while preserving the editable symbolic layout. Experiments on layout furnishing show that Architect-Ant produces geometrically valid and functionally plausible layouts, and suggest a scalable path for furnishing larger structure-only floor-plan datasets.

### [48] [Mind the Gap: Can Frontier LLMs Pass a Standardized Office Proficiency Exam?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10956)
*Tengchao Lv,Dongdong Zhang,Jiayu Ding,Yilin Jia,Yuzhong Zhao,Yupan Huang,Wenshan Wu,Xiangyang Zhou,Shaohan Huang,Nan Yang,Li Dong,Lei Cui,Furu Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文基于中国计算机等级考试（NCRE）提出了一套包含200个Office实操任务的基准测试，用于评估LLM代理在复杂办公自动化场景中的能力。结果显示，即使结合执行反馈、迭代修复等机制的最强代理系统得分仅68.8%，远低于95.5%的社区参考分数，表明当前LLM在细粒度文档自动化方面仍面临重大挑战。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM代理在专业级办公软件自动化方面的能力缺乏系统评估，Office自动化作为需要长程规划、精确参数配置和多应用集成的理想测试环境，其评估空白亟待填补。

Method: 基于中国NCRE考试构建了包含200个综合实操任务（覆盖Word/Excel/PowerPoint）的基准测试，每个任务按100分制评分，共7,118个机器可评分的评估标准。使用Score Rate (SR)作为指标，测试了7个前沿LLM及其代理系统。

Result: 单轮LLM最高得分仅36.6%；集成执行反馈、迭代修复和更广泛Office访问权限的代理系统达到68.8%，但仍远低于95.5%的社区参考分数。

Conclusion: 尽管代码生成技术取得进展，但当前LLM及代理系统在实现可靠的细粒度Office文档自动化方面仍面临显著挑战。

Abstract: The deployment of Large Language Model (LLM) agents for computer automation is accelerating, yet their ability to navigate complex, professional-grade productivity software is largely untested. We argue that Office automation is an ideal environment for benchmarking document-automation capability, as it requires long-horizon planning and reasoning, precise parameter configuration, and multi-application integration. To quantify this capability, we introduce an evaluation based on China's National Computer Rank Examination (NCRE), featuring 200 comprehensive practical-operation tasks across Word, Excel, and PowerPoint. Each task is scored on a 100-point rubric scale using 7,118 machine-gradable criteria, and Score Rate (SR) denotes the mean percentage of rubric points earned across these tasks. We benchmark 7 frontier LLMs and observe stark limitations: single-turn models score a maximum of 36.6%. A stronger agentic system with execution feedback, iterative repair, and broader Office automation access reaches 68.8%, but remains below the 95.5% community-reference score used as a scoring sanity check. Ultimately, our experiments demonstrate that despite recent advancements in code generation, achieving reliable fine-grained Office document automation remains a significant challenge for current code-generating LLM and agent systems.

### [49] [Bellman-Taylor Score Decoding for Markov Decision Processes with State-Dependent Feasible Action Sets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10979)
*Yi Chen,Rushuai Yang,Qiang Chen,Dongyan,Huo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出贝尔曼-泰勒分数解码框架，通过将策略学习迁移到欧几里得分数空间并利用动作解码器保证可行性，使得标准深度强化学习算法能够处理具有状态依赖和隐式约束动作空间的马尔可夫决策过程，并在队列网络控制问题上取得近最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 运筹学中的许多马尔可夫决策过程具有状态依赖且由各种操作约束隐式定义的可行动作，这使得标准深度强化学习算法难以直接应用，因为它们的动作接口通常假设固定的有限动作集或简单的欧几里得空间。

Method: 受最优动作价值函数的泰勒展开启发，提出贝尔曼-泰勒分数解码框架。该框架将策略学习迁移到欧几里得分数空间，通过动作解码器保证可行性，使得诱导的潜在分数MDP可以通过标准DRL算法优化，无需对解码器进行微分。

Result: 性能保证表明该方法的优化差距可分解为结构近似误差和算法学习误差。在队列网络控制问题中，策略本质上学习了状态依赖的索引式调度规则。数值实验显示小实例中近最优性能，较大系统中相比基准有显著改进。

Conclusion: 该方法有效解决了具有复杂约束动作空间的MDP问题，通过将可行动作学习转化为无约束分数空间学习，实现了标准DRL算法的直接应用，并在队列网络控制问题上验证了有效性。

Abstract: Many Markov decision processes (MDPs) in operations research have feasible actions that are state dependent and defined implicitly by various operational constraints. These features make it difficult to use standard deep reinforcement learning (DRL) algorithms, whose action interfaces typically assume either a fixed finite action catalog or a simple Euclidean space. Motivated by a Taylor expansion of the optimal action-value function, we propose Bellman--Taylor score decoding, a framework that moves policy learning to a Euclidean score space while enforcing feasibility through an action decoder. The induced latent-score MDP then can be optimized by standard DRL algorithms without differentiating through the decoder. We provide a performance guarantee showing that the optimality gap of this approach decomposes into a structural approximation error and an algorithmic learning error. Lastly, we apply this framework to a queueing network control problem, where the policy essentially learns a state-dependent index-based dispatching rule. Numerical experiments show near-optimal performance in small instances and considerable improvements over benchmarks in larger systems.

### [50] [Null-Space Constrained Low-Rank Adaptation for Response-Specified Large Language Model Unlearning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10989)
*Bocheng Ju,Jianhua Wang,Chengliang Liu,Xiaolin Chang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出NSRU，一种基于零空间约束的低秩框架，通过结构化安全目标响应、正交投影低秩参数化和联合优化目标，实现大型语言模型的可控遗忘，在TOFU和WMDP基准上有效抑制不良知识同时保持模型效用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM遗忘方法要么仅抑制不良回答而缺乏行为引导，要么在指定替代行为时对更新局部性约束不足，导致遗忘过程可能破坏模型已有的良性能力。

Method: NSRU包含三个核心组件：(1) 显式结构化的安全目标响应，为每个遗忘查询指定期望行为；(2) 从良性隐藏表示中估计逐模块的保留子空间，并通过正交投影低秩参数化将LoRA更新约束在保留子空间的零空间内；(3) 联合优化目标，同时学习安全目标、抑制不良回答并保持保留能力。

Result: 在TOFU上有效抑制可提取的遗忘知识，同时提升保留QA性能、模型效用和安全目标对齐；在WMDP上使危险领域准确率接近随机猜测区域，同时保持广泛和领域相邻的MMLU效用。消融实验验证了各组件的互补作用，敏感性和鲁棒性分析表明超参数和提示变化下行为稳定。

Conclusion: 零空间约束的投影更新能在减少保留侧扰动的同时保留编辑方向，从而实现对遗忘查询行为的有效塑造，是一种受控且局部化的LLM遗忘方法。

Abstract: Large language model unlearning aims to suppress designated undesirable knowledge while preserving benign capabilities. Many unlearning objectives focus on suppressing undesired answers, while recent target-guided variants specify replacement behavior but still leave update locality largely unconstrained. This paper introduces \emph{Null-Space Constrained Response-Specified Unlearning} (NSRU), a projection-constrained low-rank framework for controlled LLM unlearning. NSRU uses an explicitly structured safe target response to specify the desired behavior for each forget query, while suppressing the original undesired content. To localize adaptation, NSRU estimates per-module retain subspaces from benign hidden representations and uses an orthogonal-projected low-rank parameterization to confine LoRA updates to the null space of the retain subspace. The resulting objective jointly optimizes safe-target learning, undesired-response suppression, and retention preservation under this constrained parameterization. We provide a local first-order analysis showing that the projected update reduces retain-side perturbations while preserving editable directions for shaping forget-query behavior. Experiments on TOFU show that NSRU effectively suppresses extractable forget-set knowledge while improving retain QA performance, model utility, and safe-target alignment over representative baselines. On WMDP, NSRU keeps hazardous-domain accuracy near the random-choice region while preserving broad and domain-adjacent MMLU utility. Ablation studies support the complementary roles of safe-target supervision, undesired-response suppression, retention loss, and null-space projected updates, while sensitivity and robustness analyses indicate stable behavior across the tested hyperparameter and prompt variations.

### [51] [Structure from Reasoning, Numbers from Search: On-Premise Open LLMs as Structural Priors for Coupled MIMO Controller Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11015)
*Jiaxuan Chen,Haonan Li,Yang Shu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了开源大语言模型（LLM）在强耦合MIMO工业过程控制器调参中的应用，发现LLM在简单回路中无优势，但在强耦合系统中，通过提供非对称结构和可解释性，能以远少于全局优化器的样本数达到全局最优，充当样本高效、可解释的结构先验。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强耦合MIMO过程的控制器调参困难：分散式经典自整定忽视回路耦合，局部数值优化因非凸代价面而停滞。需要一种无需模型、数据保密的辅助方法。

Method: 在CSTR单回路和强耦合四水箱系统上，对比继电反馈调参、局部优化、全局优化（差分进化）与开源LLM调参。LLM通过脚手架提示（scaffolding）推理耦合特性，提出非对称控制器结构，并可选结合经典优化器精调。

Result: 单回路CSTR：继电反馈（IAE 0.106）优于LLM（0.162）。强耦合四水箱：朴素继电（J~28.6）和LLM（29.7）不如开环（22.7）；局部优化10/10失败；脚手架LLM从任意起点达J~16.9±0.2，精调后达全局最优J~12.0（10/10成功）；样本效率优势显著（18次评估 vs 全局优化器低于开环），且规模越大优势越明显（3×3系统约6倍）。

Conclusion: 开源LLM在控制调参中的价值不是作为优化器，而是作为样本高效、可解释的结构先验；良性系统中无优势，但在强耦合高维问题中边界清晰。提供了可复现基准。

Abstract: Tuning controllers for strongly coupled multi-input multi-output (MIMO) industrial processes is hard: decentralized classical auto-tuning ignores loop interaction, and local numerical optimization from natural initializations stalls in the resulting non-convex cost landscape. We ask whether on-premise open-source large language models (LLMs), which keep data on-site and need no plant model, can help. On a single-loop CSTR, classical relay-feedback tuning (IAE 0.106, near the 0.102 optimum) beats an LLM tuner (0.162): for simple loops the LLM adds nothing. The picture inverts on a strongly coupled quadruple-tank with conflicting set-points, scored by a penalized cost J = IAE + lambda*TV(u) that rewards tracking without chattering actuators. There, naive relay tuning (J ~ 28.6) and naive LLM tuning (29.7) are no better than open loop (22.7), and a local optimizer from balanced starts fails in 10/10 runs. A scaffolded open LLM instead reasons about the coupling, proposes the counter-intuitive asymmetric structure, and reaches J ~ 16.9 +/- 0.2 from any start; refining it with a classical optimizer attains the smooth global optimum (J ~ 12.0, 10/10 vs. 0/10), which even applies a non-obvious negative integral correction decentralized tuning cannot. A global optimizer (differential evolution) also reaches this optimum, so the LLM is not the only route; its advantage is sample efficiency and interpretability: a usable controller in 18 evaluations (where the global optimizer is worse than open loop) plus a stated rationale. This edge grows with dimension, reaching ~6x fewer evaluations on a 3x3 plant. The behaviour generalizes across four open models, and on a benign plant the LLM offers no advantage, sharpening the boundary. We contribute a reproducible benchmark delimiting when open LLMs help in control tuning: not as optimizers, but as a sample-efficient, interpretable structural prior.

*Gabriel Freedman,Francesca Toni*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: LLM在二元决策中表现出系统性结构（可被行为模型预测），但自我报告与真实决策驱动力不完全一致，呈现一种"浅层信念"现象——决策受属性驱动但语言化解释能力有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究LLM在二元选择任务中的决策是否具有系统性的潜在结构，还是仅仅模仿表面理由（即随机或无深层结构）。

Method: 使用合成二元决策场景（属性分级定义选项），对比模型声称最重要的属性与基于行为模型（拟合先前决策）推断出的最佳解释属性。通过保持集预测、提示顺序/采样扰动、替代行为模型、目标遮挡分析及结构变化场景进行验证。

Result: 行为模型能很好预测保留集选择，表明行为与可见属性系统相关而非随机；但自我报告和基于分数的判断仅部分恢复行为推断的驱动因素。该模式在多种扰动下保持稳定。

Conclusion: LLM决策呈现"浅层信念"特征：行为上受属性的概率性局部优先级引导，但对驱动决策的属性仅有有限的言语访问能力——输出有结构可预测，但显式理由与真实驱动力不完全匹配。

Abstract: We ask whether large language models (LLMs) merely imitate rationales when choosing between two options, or whether their choices reflect a systematic underlying decision structure. Using synthetic binary decision settings in which models choose between profiles defined by graded attributes, we compare the attribute a model says mattered most with the attribute that best explains its choice under a behavioural model fit to prior decisions. The behavioural model predicts held-out choices well, showing that model behaviour is systematically related to the visible attributes rather than being random. However, direct self-reports and a separate score-based judge recover the behaviourally inferred driver only partially. The resulting picture is neither one of arbitrary behaviour nor one of fully articulated belief - outputs are structured enough to support prediction, but explicit reasons track the recovered driver only imperfectly. This qualitative pattern persists across prompt-order and sampling perturbations, alternative behavioural models, targeted occlusion analyses, and structurally varied decision settings. We interpret this as evidence for ``superficial belief'' in LLM decision-making: models behave as if guided by probabilistic local priorities over attributes, while having only limited verbal access to the attributes that drive their decisions.

Abstract: Recent years have witnessed the rapid evolution of AI agents toward handling increasingly complex, real-world tasks. However, existing benchmarks rarely evaluate whether agents can operate graphical user interfaces to complete long-horizon, high-value professional workflows across diverse domains. Current GUI benchmarks still predominantly focus on general-purpose software, relatively simple applications, and short-horizon tasks, leaving it largely unknown whether modern agents can follow user instructions to autonomously operate domain-specific professional software and accomplish economically valuable work in an end-to-end manner. ### [54] [What Fits (Into Few Tokens) Doesn't Overfit: Compression and Generalization in ML Research Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11045)
*Martin Andres Bertran,Aaron Roth,Zhiwei Steven Wu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过LLM驱动的研究智能体实验，验证了成功机器学习策略具有高度可压缩性这一假说，即使用极短提示词或仅1比特反馈就能复现或找到高性能模型，这解释了为何自适应复用基准测试在实践中很少导致过拟合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究为何在基准测试驱动下自适应复用hold-out验证集很少导致过拟合，验证"成功策略高度可压缩"这一假说。

Method: 设计两类信息瓶颈实验：(1)输出压缩——探索智能体在验证集上搜索高性能模型，复现智能体仅凭极短提示词和训练数据尝试复现其性能；(2)输入压缩——探索智能体仅接收每位提交模型是否优于当前最优的1比特反馈。在表格分类、视觉、语言建模、扩散建模、奖励建模等8个数据集上进行测试。

Result: 信息瓶颈对性能影响很小，短提示词和可压缩反馈足以复现和找到高性能模型。当故意诱导验证集过拟合时，短提示词无法复现结果。

Conclusion: 支持描述长度解释：成功策略位于策略空间的低复杂度区域，因此自适应复用基准测试在实践中很少导致过拟合。

Abstract: Reusing a held-out benchmark adaptively should, in principle, invite overfitting. Yet benchmark-driven machine learning (ML) has produced surprisingly little overfitting in practice. An attractive hypothesis is that successful ML strategies are highly compressible. We study this in the setting of LLM-driven research agents, where the hypothesis becomes directly testable via two complementary information bottlenecks. In \emph{output compression}, an exploration agent adaptively searches for high-performance models using a validation set, and we test whether a fresh ``reproducer agent'' can reproduce its performance given only an extremely short prompt and the training data. In \emph{input compression}, the explorer receives only one-bit feedback indicating whether each submitted model improves on the running best. Across 8 datasets spanning tabular classification, vision, language modeling, diffusion modeling, and reward modeling, we find that these bottlenecks have little effect on performance: short prompts and compressible feedback are sufficient to reproduce and find high-performance models. The hypothesis is falsifiable: when we deliberately induce validation-set overfitting, the results fail to reproduce with short prompts. Taken together, our results support a description-length explanation for the lack of overfitting in benchmark-driven ML: successful strategies occupy a low-complexity region of strategy space.

### [55] [CIAware-Bench: Benchmarking Control Intervention Awareness Across Frontier LLMs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11063)
*Joachim Schaeffer,Thomas Jiralerspong,Alexander Panfilov,Guillaume Lajoie,Jonas Geiping,Yoshua Bengio,Roland S. Zimmermann*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出CIAware-Bench基准，用于评估前沿模型对控制干预（CI）的感知能力——即模型能否区分自身轨迹与被控制协议修改后的轨迹。在四个任务域上评估11种前沿模型，发现CI感知能力普遍较低至中等（最高0.87），且随任务域、模型对而变化，表明CI感知并非模型的固定属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在AI控制协议中，可信模型会监控并修改不可信模型的不安全步骤，但这种干预可能被不可信模型检测到，从而使其推断出监控器的特性并适应以逃避控制。因此需要系统评估模型对控制干预的感知能力，以设计更难被检测到的控制协议。

Method: 构建CIAware-Bench基准，包含四个任务域（essay writing、BigCodeBench、Bash Arena、SHADE-Arena），通过变化轨迹水印、侧任务存在性和控制协议，测试模型能否区分自身轨迹与被干预修改后的轨迹。

Result: 在默认设置下，11种前沿模型的CI感知能力为低至中等（最高0.87，随机基线为0.5），不同任务域和模型对之间差异显著；跨模型家族的检测通常更容易，表明模型利用了提供商特定的风格或后训练差异。

Conclusion: CI感知能力并非模型的固定属性，应针对每个新模型发布和部署场景进行测量；发布CIAware-Bench以跟踪CI感知能力，并指导设计更难被检测到的控制协议。

Abstract: AI control protocols oversee untrusted models by monitoring their actions and modifying potentially unsafe steps, often using a trusted model. This partially tampers with the untrusted model's trajectory. If the trusted model detects such an intervention, it may infer properties of the monitor and adapt to evade control. We introduce \textbf{CIAware-Bench}, a benchmark for measuring \textbf{c}ontrol \textbf{i}ntervention (CI) awareness across frontier models. CIAware-Bench tests whether models can distinguish their own trajectories from those modified by a control intervention. The benchmark is comprised of a suite of four task domains (essay writing, BigCodeBench, Bash Arena, and SHADE-Arena), while varying trajectory watermarking, side-task presence, and the control protocol. Evaluating eleven frontier models, we find low to moderate CI awareness under default settings (up to 0.87; random chance balanced binary classification accuracy is 0.5) with substantial variation across task domains and model pairs. Detection is generally easier across model families, suggesting that models exploit provider-specific differences in style or post-training. Overall, CI awareness is not a fixed model-level property, and should be measured for each new model release and deployment scenario. We release CIAware-Bench to track CI awareness and inform control protocols whose interventions are harder to detect.

</details>


### [56] [A History-Aware Visually Grounded Critic for Computer Use Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11078)
*Jaewoo Lee,Zaid Khan,Archiki Prasad,Justin Chih-Yao Chen,Supriyo Chakraborty,Kartik Balasubramaniam,Sambit Sahu,Elias Stengel-Eskin,Hyunji Lee,Mohit Bansal*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: HiViG是一个面向计算机使用代理(CUA)的测试时框架，通过历史感知的多模态批评模型和视觉接地评估，在跨平台GUI任务中显著提升成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有CUA批评模型存在两个关键局限：(1)短视决策循环，易遗忘早期操作；(2)缺乏视觉接地能力，无法检测错误操作（如点击错误UI元素）。

Method: 提出HiViG框架，核心是一个在真实GUI轨迹上训练的多模态批评模型。该模型通过宏动作历史摘要化已完成成就，并提供视觉接地批评，在预执行阶段验证原始执行坐标与当前屏幕截图。

Result: 在Web、移动端和桌面端基准测试中，HiViG一致超越现有标量批评和言语批评模型。相比最强基线，Qwen3-VL-32B提升5.8%，Gemini-3-Flash提升9.0%，并展现出强大的跨平台泛化能力。

Conclusion: 宏动作历史可缓解短视规划问题，视觉接地批评可减少执行错误，两个组件对于长视界GUI任务的测试时扩展均至关重要。

Abstract: Various test-time interventions for Computer Use Agents (CUAs), including critic models, have been developed to improve performance through pre-execution action evaluation in complex Graphical User Interface (GUI) environments. However, existing critics suffer from two key limitations: they (1) focus primarily on short-sighted decision loops (e.g., forgetting earlier actions) and (2) lack the visual grounding needed to detect flawed actions (e.g., clicking wrong UI elements). To address these, we introduce HiViG, a History-aware Visually Grounded test-time framework, built around a multimodal critic trained on real GUI trajectories to abstract past interactions into a compact record and to evaluate actions with visual grounding. At test time, HiViG integrates the critic into the policy decision loop to provide macro-action history, which summarizes the policy's completed achievements, and visually grounded critique, which verifies raw execution coordinates against the current screenshot to intercept errors before execution. Across web, mobile, and desktop benchmarks, HiViG consistently outperforms existing scalar and verbal critics, improving average success rates over the strongest baseline by 5.8% for Qwen3-VL-32B and 9.0% for Gemini-3-Flash, and demonstrates strong cross-platform generalization. Ablations show that macro-action history mitigates short-sighted planning and visually grounded critique reduces execution errors, with both components being critical for test-time scaling in long-horizon GUI tasks.

</details>


### [57] [Monte Carlo Pass Search: Using Trajectory Generation for 3D Counterfactual Pass Evaluation in Football](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11120)
*Andrew Kang,Priya Narasimhan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出蒙特卡洛传球搜索（MCPS），将足球传球评估重新定义为蒙特卡洛树搜索（MCTS）问题，利用德国足球甲级联赛的高保真3D追踪数据，结合价值模型、世界模型和反事实策略，通过分布感知的传球归因方法实现传球质量评估，并开源了模型和代码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有足球传球评估方法缺乏对反事实场景的合理建模，且缺乏高保真3D球轨迹数据支持。作者希望将传球评估形式化为MCTS问题，利用首次公开的德甲3D球轨迹数据，实现更准确的传球价值归因。

Method: 方法包括：(1) 推断每个观测传球的踢球参数；(2) 采样执行变体和选项变体；(3) 使用球条件世界模型前向推演每个候选传球至下次球交互；(4) 用学习到的价值模型评分，获得价值分布；(5) 基于均值和百分位数设计两种互补的执行盈余分数进行归因分析；(6) 采用自动驾驶领域的离散令牌自回归轨迹生成器SMART以提高样本效率。

Result: 在有限的公开数据下，SMART适配后的世界模型在前20名最佳预测准确度上优于基线方法，并且支持完全假设性的轨迹推演用于下游评估。

Conclusion: MCPS通过将传球评估形式化为分布感知的MCTS问题，结合高保真数据和跨领域轨迹生成模型，为足球数据分析提供了更精细的传球价值归因框架，代码和模型已开源。

Abstract: We recast pass evaluation in football (soccer) as a Monte Carlo Tree Search (MCTS)-like evaluation problem whose components mostly exist in the literature under different names: a value model (possession value), a world model (multi-agent trajectories with ball interactions), and a policy over counterfactual actions (sampling pass variants with noise). Building on the first public high-fidelity tracking dataset with 3D ball trajectories from the Bundesliga, we introduce Monte Carlo Pass Search (MCPS), which infers kick parameters for each observed pass, samples execution variants and option variants, rolls each candidate forward with a ball-conditioned world model until the next ball interaction, and scores outcomes with a learned value model to obtain a distribution over gained value. This distribution enables distribution-aware attribution with two complementary execution-surplus scores used for analysis and ranking: mean-based and percentile-based scores. To make the world model sample-efficient under limited public data, we adapt a discrete-token, autoregressive trajectory generator from autonomous driving (SMART) and show it yields strong best-of-20 forecasting accuracy compared to baselines, while supporting fully hypothetical rollouts for downstream evaluation. We have released model checkpoints and code.

</details>

Abstract: Large language models (LLMs) are rapidly acquiring capabilities relevant to biological research, from literature synthesis to interpretation of experimental data. Increasingly, LLM agents can also perform in silico biology tasks that previously required experienced human biologists. These emerging AI capabilities offer new opportunities for scientific discovery and biomedical advances, but they also shift the landscape of biosecurity risks. To address this, we introduce the Agentic Bio-Capabilities Benchmark (ABC-Bench), a suite of tasks to measure agentic biosecurity-relevant capabilities. ABC-Bench evaluates LLM agents on both benign and dual-use biology tasks: writing code to operate liquid handling robots, designing DNA fragments for in vitro assembly, and evading DNA synthesis screening. These tasks require a combination of biology and software expertise. All tested LLM agents outperformed the median expert human baseliner on all three tasks. Agents performed highly on tasks drawing on published knowledge and well-documented protocols, and more weakly on a task requiring novel bioinformatics reasoning. In three wet-lab validation experiments, we found that OpenAI's o4-mini-high produced scripts that, when run on an OpenTrons liquid handling robot, successfully assembled DNA with expected sequences.

### [59] [ReasonAlloc: Hierarchical Decoding-Time KV Cache Budget Allocation for Reasoning Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11164)
*Wenhao Liu,Hao Shi,Yunhe Li,Weizhi Fei,Xiangyuan Wang,Mengzhe Ruan,Hanxu Hou,Peisong Wang,Linqi Song,Shuang Qiu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ReasonAlloc是一种无训练框架，通过分层预算分配（离线层级预分配+在线头级重分配）解决长思维链推理中KV缓存增长导致的推理瓶颈，在数学推理基准上优于均匀预算的基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长思维链推理中KV缓存快速增长导致严重推理瓶颈；现有解码时压缩方法对层和注意力头采用统一预算分配，而静态非均匀预算分配方法无法捕捉自回归推理的逐步上下文需求。

Method: ReasonAlloc将解码时KV压缩建模为分层预算分配问题：离线层级预分配捕捉架构驱动的"推理波"模式；在线头级策略根据实时效用将资源重新分配给信息量大的注意力头。

Result: 在MATH-500和AIME 2024基准测试上，使用三种模型（DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B等）评估，ReasonAlloc在128-512 tokens的小预算下增益最大，超越R-KV、SnapKV和Pyramid-RKV等基线方法。

Conclusion: ReasonAlloc可即插即用集成到现有token驱逐策略中，引入的推理时开销可忽略不计。

Abstract: Long chain-of-thought (CoT) trajectories in large language model (LLM) reasoning cause severe inference bottlenecks due to rapid key-value (KV) cache growth. Current decoding-time compression methods mitigate this issue via token eviction, but typically assume a uniform budget distribution across all layers and heads. In contrast, existing non-uniform budget allocation methods are predominantly designed for the static prompt prefill phase, and they do not capture the stepwise context demands of autoregressive reasoning. To bridge this gap, we propose ReasonAlloc, a training-free framework that recasts decoding-time KV compression as a hierarchical budget allocation problem. ReasonAlloc operates at two complementary levels: an offline layer-wise preallocation strategy captures an architecture-driven demand pattern which we call ``\textit{Reasoning Wave}'', while an online head-wise strategy reallocates resources during decoding to information-rich heads based on real-time utility. Evaluations on mathematical reasoning benchmarks (MATH-500, AIME~2024) using DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Llama-8B, DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen-14B, and AceReason-14B show that ReasonAlloc outperforms uniform-budget R-KV, SnapKV, and Pyramid-RKV (a baseline enforcing a static, monotonically decreasing layer budget), with the largest gains at small budgets (128-512 tokens). ReasonAlloc is plug-and-play with existing token-eviction policies and introduces negligible inference-time overhead.

</details>


### [60] [The Role of Feedback Alignment in Self-Distillation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11173)
*Semih Kara,Oğuzhan Ersoy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了自蒸馏中上下文设计的影响，发现与求解器推理轨迹对齐的逐步批评（step-aligned critique）作为自教师上下文效果最佳，显著优于二元奖励和参考答案条件，原因在于它能精准定位错误token而不干扰正确推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自蒸馏通过匹配有/无上下文的模型输出分布来提升性能，但自教师接收的上下文设计尚未被系统探索。本文旨在研究不同上下文设计对自蒸馏效果的影响。

Method: 在冻结评判器提供反馈的条件下训练求解器，比较三种上下文条件：(i) 二元奖励（GRPO），(ii) 参考答案，(iii) 与求解器推理轨迹对齐的逐步批评。通过每token优势分析解释不同条件的效果差异。

Result: 逐步对齐批评效果最佳，在Avg@12上分别超过GRPO 16.11分、超过参考答案条件5.27分。参考答案条件会在每个token（包括正确步骤）施加更改压力，而逐步对齐反馈仅针对推理失败token。

Conclusion: 反馈与求解器推理的结构对齐是自蒸馏效果的关键驱动因素。

Abstract: Conditioning a language model on additional context, such as feedback on a previous attempt, typically improves its response. Self-distillation trains the model to retain this improvement when the context is not present. The method works by matching the model's output distribution under two settings: a student that sees only the question, and a self-teacher that also sees the context. What the model learns therefore depends on what context the self-teacher receives, yet the design of this context remains largely unexplored.
  We study context design for self-distillation by training a solver on feedback from a frozen critic. We compare three conditions: (i) a binary reward (GRPO), (ii) the reference solution, and (iii) a step-by-step critique aligned to the solver's reasoning trace.
  Step-aligned critique yields the largest gains, outperforming GRPO by 16.11 points and reference-solution-conditioned self-distillation by 5.27 points (Avg@12). Per-token advantage analysis reveals why: step-aligned feedback targets only the tokens where reasoning fails, leaving correct behavior intact. Conditioning on the reference solution, by contrast, pressures the model to change its behavior at every token (even correct steps) because an alternative derivation inevitably differs in phrasing and approach. This suggests that structural alignment between feedback and the solver's reasoning is a key driver of self-distillation effectiveness.

</details>

### [61] [Anomaly Detection and Root Cause Analysis for Microservice Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09942)
*Luan Pham*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本论文针对微服务系统异常检测与根因分析（RCA）中存在的五大局限性（检测与RCA分离、事件数据未充分利用、依赖服务调用图、缺少标准化基准、因果推断方法评估不清晰），提出了两组贡献：第一组包括BARO（端到端异常检测与RCA）、EventADL（事件数据框架）和TORAI（无需服务调用图的多模态RCA）；第二组包括RCAEval基准数据集与系统评估框架。实验验证了方法的有效性和鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微服务系统故障会导致用户体验下降和经济损失，现有异常检测与RCA技术存在五大局限：检测与RCA分离导致鲁棒性差、事件数据未被充分利用、依赖服务调用图、缺乏标准化评估框架、因果推断方法的有效性不明确。

Method: 提出两组贡献：1) BARO（基于指标数据的端到端异常检测与RCA）、EventADL（面向事件数据的端到端框架）、TORAI（无需服务调用图的多模态RCA框架）；2) RCAEval基准数据集与评估框架，以及对现有RCA方法（特别是因果推断方法）的系统评估。

Result: 在真实微服务系统上的广泛实验验证了BARO、EventADL和TORAI的有效性和鲁棒性；RCAEval提供了可直接使用的数据集和可复现的基线；系统评估为因果推断方法提供了指导性见解。

Conclusion: 本论文推动了微服务故障的自动化异常检测与根因分析领域发展，为未来的事件缓解和修复研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: Microservice systems are widely used to build cloud applications, yet their complexity makes failures inevitable, degrading user experience and causing economic loss. Automated anomaly detection and root cause analysis (RCA) are now active research areas, but existing techniques share five limitations. First, most treat anomaly detection and RCA separately, assuming anomalies are detected correctly, and falter when detection is imprecise due to noise or delay. Second, they focus on metrics, logs, and traces, leaving event data such as API calls and configuration changes underexplored. Third, many require a given service call graph and cannot diagnose without one. Fourth, the field lacks standardised datasets and evaluation frameworks, so methods are hard to compare fairly. Fifth, although causal inference-based RCA has become dominant, its effectiveness, efficiency, and robustness remain unclear.
  This thesis addresses these limitations through two groups of contributions. The first introduces methods that exploit observability data both independently and collectively. BARO is an end-to-end anomaly detection and RCA approach for metric data. EventADL is an end-to-end framework for event data. TORAI is a multimodal RCA framework that requires no service call graph. Extensive experiments on real microservice systems demonstrate their effectiveness and robustness. The second group delivers benchmarking datasets, an evaluation framework, and systematic evaluation efforts. RCAEval is a comprehensive benchmark providing ready-to-use datasets and reproducible baselines for future research. A systematic evaluation of existing RCA methods, especially causal inference-based approaches, offers insights that guide future directions. This thesis thereby advances automated anomaly detection and RCA for microservice failures, enabling future research on incident mitigation and remediation.

</details>

*Nikolai Rozanov*

Main category: cs.SE

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (1) 令牌对齐算法解决跨模型tokenization不匹配问题；(2) 轻量级多任务LLM（MLC）用于行级bug分类；(3) 优化的多行预测训练策略。

Abstract: The rapid adoption of LLM-powered code generation has dramatically accelerated software development, yet effective verification methods remain severely underdeveloped. Existing bug localization techniques are either prohibitively expensive, requiring minutes of agentic reasoning and thousands of generated tokens per file, and/or operate at coarse function-level granularity unsuitable for precise debugging. While works that focus on line-level granularity and are more light-weight are often limited in their performance or context size. We introduce a novel line-level bug localization approach that addresses these limitations through three key contributions: (1) a token alignment algorithm that overcomes fundamental tokenization challenges in previous work, (2) a lightweight multi-task LLM for bug localization (MLC) enabling efficient line-level bug classification, and (3) an optimized training recipe for multi-line prediction. Our method achieves state-of-the-art performance among similar setups on line-level bug localization with full-file context. At the same time we reach comparable performance to agentic approaches on Defects4J and PypiBugs benchmarks while reducing inference latency by orders of magnitudes, requiring only a single generated token per file. We further demonstrate strong generalization by introducing and evaluating on a small out-of-domain evaluation datasets in Python. We will open source our code, models, and datasets upon acceptance.

We propose a novel data-aware static analysis approach to detect semantic faults in machine learning code, allowing developers to reveal these bugs while writing code instead of after training the model. ### [64] [What makes a harness a harness: necessary and sufficient conditions for an agent harness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10106)
*Sanderson Oliveira de Macedo*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过概念分析，为软件工程中生成式AI领域的"agent harness"（代理框架/脚手架）术语提供了一个可操作的定义，包括其充要条件、包含/排除测试，并将其与代理框架、SDK、IDE插件、评估脚手架和编排器进行了边界划分。研究还将该术语从马具到测试脚手架再到机器学习评估脚手架的词源学谱系进行了重构，并基于六个真实系统（Claude Code、Codex CLI、Aider、Cline、OpenHands、SWE-agent）验证了定义的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: "agent harness"一词在软件工程和生成式AI领域使用松散且多义——有时指整个产品（如Claude Code、Codex CLI），有时指评估脚手架（如SWE-bench harness），有时又与代理框架、SDK、IDE插件或编排器混为一谈。亟需一个能够一致地包含和排除案例的参考定义，以指导工程实践和科学比较。

Method: 采用概念分析方法，结合具有持久标识符的学术文献和主要灰色文献（官方文档、术语表、工程报告），重构术语的词源学谱系。提出构成性定义，规定充要条件，并将其操作化为包含/排除测试，对六个真实harness和边缘案例进行应用验证。

Result: 给出了agent harness的构成性定义（充要条件）和操作化的包含/排除测试；该定义在Claude Code、Codex CLI、Aider、Cline、OpenHands、SWE-agent六个真实系统以及精心设计的边缘案例上表现出一致的包含/排除能力；明确了agent harness与代理框架、代理SDK、IDE插件、评估脚手架、编排器之间的概念边界。

Conclusion: 贡献是一个可操作的agent harness定义和共享词汇表，能够指导工程实践和智能体系统的科学比较。未来工作以设计张力轴线的形式组织为一个研究议程。

Abstract: The term agent harness now circulates widely in software engineering with generative artificial intelligence. It names the layer that wraps a language model and turns it into a coding agent able to act on a repository. The usage is loose and polysemous. Sometimes the term denotes the whole product (Claude Code, Codex CLI); sometimes it denotes the evaluation scaffold that runs an agent against tasks (the SWE-bench harness); sometimes it gets conflated with an agent framework, an SDK, an IDE plugin, or an orchestrator. What is missing is a reference definition that works as an instrument, one that includes and excludes cases consistently. We build that definition through a conceptual analysis that combines works with persistent identifiers and primary grey-literature sources, such as official documentation, glossaries, and engineering reports. We reconstruct the genealogy of the term, from the horse's tack to the classic test harness, to the machine-learning evaluation harness, and finally to the agent harness. We then propose a constitutive definition that states the necessary and sufficient conditions for a system to be an agent harness, we operationalize it as an inclusion and exclusion test, and we draw the boundary of the concept against an agent framework, an agent SDK, an IDE plugin, an eval harness, and an orchestrator. We apply the definition to six real harnesses (Claude Code, Codex CLI, Aider, Cline, OpenHands, and SWE-agent) and to deliberate edge cases; the test includes and excludes consistently. We close with a research agenda organized by design tension axes. The contribution is an operational definition of agent harness, with a shared vocabulary, able to guide engineering practice and the scientific comparison of agentic systems.

</details>


### [65] [TestMap: Evidence Infrastructure for Foundation-Model-Assisted Test Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10211)
*Hunter Leary,Luke Hanuska,Chris Brown*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出TestMap，一个开源基础设施原型，用于自动化C#/.NET仓库中基于基础模型的测试生成、验证与追踪，记录每个生成候选项的完整生命周期（包括失败、修复、低影响和证据阳性结果），而不仅仅是最终通过的测试。

Method: TestMap作为一个开源基础设施原型，支持仓库分析、源代码-测试映射、基线执行、代码度量收集、测试气味检测、覆盖率测量、变异测试、模型引导的测试生成、验证、修复以及仓库特定的实验追踪。系统不仅记录最终通过的测试，还追踪每个生成候选项的完整生命周期。

Result: 通过记录失败、修复、低影响和证据阳性等中间结果，TestMap能够揭示模型局限性、缺失上下文、修复成本、工具链低效或被测系统中的潜在故障。

Abstract: Foundation models (FMs) can generate plausible unit tests, but determining whether those tests are correct, useful, maintainable, and worth integrating remains difficult. Generated tests must be mapped to the code they target, inserted into real projects, built, executed, measured against the baseline suite, repaired when necessary, and compared across models and generation strategies. This validation process is fragmented across build systems, test runners, coverage tools, mutation tools, static analyzers, and experiment scripts. The problem is especially important because generated tests are both code artifacts and validation artifacts: they must themselves be validated before they can be trusted as evidence about the system under test. This paper presents TestMap, an open-source infrastructure prototype that automates evidence-backed foundation-model-assisted test generation for C#/.NET repositories. TestMap supports repository analysis, source-test mapping, baseline execution, code metric collection, test smell detection, coverage measurement, mutation testing, model-guided test generation, validation, repair, and repository-specific experiment tracking. Rather than reporting only final passing tests, TestMap records the lifecycle of each generated candidate, including failed, repaired, low-impact, and evidence positive outcomes. These intermediate outcomes can reveal model limitations, missing context, repair cost, toolchain inefficiencies, or possible faults in the system under test. Using TestMap as a design case, we describe the architecture and evidence model needed to make generated tests observable, repeatable, and comparable across repositories, models, prompts, and generation strategies. We conclude with lessons learned and open challenges, including oracle and assertion quality, metric attribution, test maintainability, flakiness, execution cost, and developer acceptance.

### [68] [Beyond Coverage and Kill Scores: Empirically Measuring Test Suite Behavioural Gaps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10417)
*Partha Protim Paul,Reid Holmes*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出一种自动化方法，从自然语言文档和源代码中提取方法级预期行为，将其映射到现有测试用例，从而识别测试套件与预期行为之间的缺口（即"行为缺口"）。在10个开源Java库上的评估表明，17.5%的预期行为未被测试覆盖，且传统结构指标（行覆盖、变异测试）无法预测这些缺口，说明行为覆盖是独立于传统指标的测试充分性维度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统测试充分性指标（代码覆盖、变异测试）仅衡量实现层面，无法检测代码实际行为与预期行为之间的偏差，而此前缺乏可靠方法来自动识别这些偏差。

Method: 从自然语言文档和源代码中提取方法级预期行为，将其映射到现有测试用例，通过比对识别出未被验证的预期行为。

Result: 在10个开源Java库（8,922个方法）中提取20,729个行为，精度93.1%；17.5%的预期行为完全未被测试覆盖；EVOSUITE和ASTER分别遗漏20.6%和27.1%的预期行为；大多数未测试行为出现在高行覆盖率的方法中，超过半数出现在高变异得分的方法中。

Conclusion: 行为覆盖是一种独立于传统结构指标（行覆盖、变异测试）的测试充分性维度，能够补充现有测试评估体系。

Abstract: Traditional test adequacy metrics measure a system's implementation, not whether it adheres to its expected behaviour. While developers rely heavily on code coverage and mutation testing to assess test suite quality, these metrics are fundamentally implementation-centric and cannot detect gaps between what the code is expected to do and what it actually does. Unfortunately, there has been no way to reliably detect these discrepancies; in this paper we introduce an automated proof-of-concept approach to investigate these gaps. The approach extracts expected method-level behaviours from natural language documentation and source code, maps them to existing test cases, and identifies gaps between expected and validated behaviours. We evaluate the approach across ten popular open-source Java libraries comprising 8,922 methods, extracting 20,729 behaviours with 93.1% precision. Our empirical analysis conservatively estimates that 17.5% of detected expected behaviours remain entirely untested, which we term as the test suite's behavioural gap. To determine if these gaps are merely an artifact of human-driven testing, we evaluate state-of-the-art automated test generators (EVOSUITE / ASTER), finding that they similarly fail to validate at least 20.6% / 27.1% of detected expected behaviours. We further demonstrate that behavioural gaps are not predicted by traditional structural metrics: the majority of untested behaviours occur in methods that already have high line coverage, and over half persist in methods with high mutation kill score. These results suggest behavioural coverage acts as an independent dimension of test suite adequacy that can complement traditional structural metrics.

### [69] [MASTOR: A Multi-Agent Approach to Semantic Test Oracle Generation for RESTful APIs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10465)
*Sida Deng,Rubing Huang,Zhenzhen Yang,Man Zhang,Xuan Xie,Rongcun Wang*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 提出MASTOR，一种基于多智能体的RESTful API语义测试预言生成方法，通过分析实现源码构建上下文，生成状态/字段预言和行为一致性预言，在13个开源项目上平均变异得分75.4%，显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RESTful API自动化测试方法仅依赖HTTP状态码和模式一致性等简单检查，无法检测语义错误、业务逻辑违规和状态依赖不一致等问题。

Method: 两阶段方法：1) 源码分析阶段，通过源码提取智能体分析传递导入闭包构建每个端点操作的源码上下文；2) 预言生成阶段，包含单操作路径（生成状态和字段预言）和多操作路径（通过跨操作语义关联生成行为一致性预言），结合挑战者智能体评审机制和预言归一化过滤。

Result: 在13个开源项目（296个操作，251,303行代码）上平均变异得分75.4%，生成10,022个预言；在50个操作对比中，MASTOR分别超过Direct Prompting 30.1个百分点（69.9% vs 39.8%）和SATORI 49.4个百分点（69.9% vs 20.5%）。

Conclusion: MASTOR通过多智能体协作和源码分析的结合，能有效生成语义丰富的测试预言，显著提升RESTful API测试的缺陷检测能力。

Abstract: Existing automated RESTful API testing approaches commonly rely on simple checks (e.g., HTTP status codes, schema conformance), which are insufficient for detecting semantic faults, business logic violations, and state-dependent inconsistencies. To address this, we propose MASTOR, a Multi-Agent approach for generating Semantic Test Oracles for RESTful APIs based on implementation source code. MASTOR consists of two phases: source analysis and oracle generation. The former employs a source extraction agent to construct a source context for each endpoint operation by analyzing a transitive import closure of relevant source files. The latter employs two parallel oracle-generation paths over the collected contexts: a single-operation path producing status and field oracles per operation, and a multi-operation path generating behavioral consistency oracles for operation sequences by leveraging cross-operation semantic associations. Both paths apply a challenger-agent review, where a dedicated reviewer identifies weaknesses and issues improvement hints to guide targeted regeneration, followed by oracle normalization to filter out structurally invalid oracles. We evaluated MASTOR on a benchmark of 13 open-source RESTful API projects (296 operations, 251,303 lines of code) from the WFD and PRAB datasets. MASTOR achieved an average mutation score of 75.4%, generating 10,022 oracles. These oracles were translated into executable assertions via ToJUnit and ToPostmanAssertify, and into human-readable descriptions via ToReadable. In a baseline comparison on 50 selected operations, MASTOR outperformed Direct Prompting by 30.1 percentage points (69.9% vs. 39.8%) and SATORI by 49.4 percentage points (69.9% vs. 20.5%).

To address this, we propose an intent driven requirements completion approach that reframes rule completion as a dual process: reconstructing intent from fragmented rules, then regenerating rules from that intent, with safety embedded throughout. We introduce a Bidirectional Requirements Traceability Tree, a three layer model linking rules, intents, and quality concerns, and design a multiagent framework that combines LLM reasoning with structured traceability. This enables completions that are both functionally complete and inherently safe, while remaining traceable and explainable. Evaluation shows our method significantly outperforms the baselines, improving the rule completion rate by 43% and reducing logical conflicts by over 21%. By grounding completion in intent understanding, we shift the paradigm from user to system responsibility, and from functional correctness to holistic trustworthiness.

Goal: We propose a confirmatory empirical study correlating Self-Admitted Technical Debt (SATD) with hardware-level runtime energy consumption across agentic frameworks, to determine whether code quality can drive energy-aware design decisions. Method: We will evaluate five open-source agentic frameworks by executing a standardized task suite in a strictly controlled environment. ### [72] [DeNovoSWE: Scaling Long-Horizon Environments for Generating Entire Repositories from Scratch](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10728)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: As the capabilities of LLM-based code agents continue to advance, their expected role is expanding beyond localized bug fixing in existing codebases toward architecting and implementing complete software repositories from high-level specifications. However, training agents for such long-horizon software engineering tasks remains difficult due to the scarcity of large-scale, verifiable whole-repository generation data. In this paper, we introduce \textbf{DeNovoSWE}, a large-scale dataset for whole-repository generation. DeNovoSWE comprises 4,818 high-quality instances, where each instance requires generating a complete repository from documentation. Our dataset is automatically constructed through a carefully designed sandboxed agentic workflow, enabling scalable curation without human annotation. DeNovoSWE is constructed with "divide and conquer" and critic-repair philosophy. To balance data quality and diversity, we further introduce a difficulty-aware trajectory filtering strategy. Fine-tuning Qwen3-30B-A3B on DeNovoSWE substantially improves long-horizon SWE performance, raising its score on the challenging BeyondSWE-Doc2Repo benchmark from 5.8% to 47.2%.

### [74] [From Perception to Action: Can UI Interventions Foster Sustainable LLM Chatbot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.10861)
*Nitish Patkar,Pooja Rani,Jack Glässer,Simon Lüscher,Martin Kropp*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究了可持续导向的UI干预措施（如模式切换、能耗反馈等）能否提升用户对AI能源消耗的 awareness 并促进更节能的聊天机器人使用行为。基线调查（n=77）显示用户认知不足但关注度高，田野实验（n=11, 5天）表明节能模式使用占比55.8%，模式切换是主要行为机制。结论：UI层干预可有效补充后端效率优化，支持更节能的LLM交互。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 基线调查：94.8%受访者声称对AI能耗有认知，但88.3%误估实际消耗；仅39.0%愿为省能接受性能折损。田野实验：节能模式占全部提示的55.8%，90.9%自我报告在无需高精度场景主动选择节能模式；用户未缩短提示长度，模式切换为主要行为改变机制。

Conclusion: 可持续导向的UI干预能够提升用户能源意识并支持更节能的LLM聊天机器人交互模式。这些效果应被理解为行为层面和基于模型的估算，可补充后端效率优化工作。提供的原型和复制包支持未来能源感知对话式AI设计研究。

Abstract: LLM-powered chatbots are increasingly embedded in everyday workflows, raising sustainability concerns due to their energy use. Most mitigation strategies emphasize model or infrastructure efficiency, while the user-interface (UI) layer remains underexplored despite its potential to shape interaction behavior. We investigate whether sustainability-oriented UI interventions can increase users' energy awareness and encourage more energy-responsible chatbot use without reducing usability. Guided by prior work on persuasive technology and choice architecture, we implemented a web-based chatbot prototype with a three-mode switch (Energy-efficient, Balanced, Performance), per-response energy feedback, pre-send energy estimates, a usage metrics dashboard, and energy analogies. We then evaluated the prototype in a five-day field study with 11 participants. In the baseline survey, 94.8% of respondents reported at least some awareness of AI energy use, yet 88.3% misestimated actual consumption. Although concern about environmental impact was high, only 39.0% indicated willingness to accept a performance trade-off for lower energy use. In the field study, Energy-efficient mode accounted for 55.8% of logged prompts, while 90.9% self-reported actively choosing Eco-mode when high accuracy was not required. Participants did not reduce prompt length, suggesting mode switching as the primary behavioral mechanism. Sustainability-oriented UI interventions can improve awareness and support more energy-responsible interaction patterns in LLM chatbots. These effects are best interpreted as behavioral and model-based estimates that complement backend efficiency work, and the provided prototype and replication package support further research on energy-aware conversational AI design.

### [78] [GapFuzz: Cross-Plane Divergence Fuzzing for Distributed SDN Controllers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11035)
*Moustapha Awwalou Diouf,Samuel Ouya,Jacques Klein,Tegawendé F. Bissyandé*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: GapFuzz是一个针对分布式SDN集群的有状态并发模糊测试工具，通过在主备节点间注入矛盾的北向请求并探测控制平面与内核数据平面状态，发现81.7%的尝试会产生发散裁决（即集群权威状态与内核数据路径不一致）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分布式SDN集群中异步复制流状态会在主备节点间留下时间窗口，导致两个备份节点可能提交矛盾规则、主节点将两者序列化到数据平面、内核数据路径锁定在无节点认为权威的动作上。现有SDN模糊测试器局限在控制平面、针对单一控制器或未引导并发以触发复制竞争，无法发现此类故障。

Method: GapFuzz在两个非主节点上以受控注入间延迟Δt注入矛盾的北向请求对；通过ovs-appctl ofproto/trace查询每个副本和内核数据路径动作重构全局跨平面状态；两阶段时序搜索检测发散是否存在，然后对Δt进行加倍和二分定位注入时间窗口；生命周期探测标记每个裁决是瞬时还是持久，并将其归入源于ONOS 2.7源码的四类跨平面状态之一。

Result: 在三节点ONOS 2.7集群上，GapFuzz在81.7%的尝试中产生发散裁决（N=50, Wilson 95% CI [77.3, 85.4]%）；所有发散都位于集群权威状态与内核数据路径之间。第二阶段将一个模板的5 ms竞争窗口与六个模板的加倍捕获区间（Δt_max=10.24 s）区分开，99.4%的发散持续超过30秒。用先前模糊测试器使用的OpenFlow用户空间探测替换内核数据路径探测后，整体检测率下降26.6个百分点，排除规范化强制裁决后下降46.5个百分点。

Conclusion: GapFuzz有效证明了分布式SDN集群中存在跨平面状态发散漏洞，且该漏洞无法被仅关注控制平面的现有方法检测到；跨平面状态探测（尤其是内核数据路径探测）对于发现此类并发复制竞争至关重要。

Abstract: Distributed Software-Defined Networking (SDN) clusters replicate flow state asynchronously between a master node and its backups, leaving a window during which two backup nodes can each commit a contradictory rule, the master can serialize both into the data plane, and the kernel datapath can latch onto an action that no node believes authoritative. Existing SDN fuzzers miss this fault: they confine their oracle to the control plane, target a single controller, or do not steer concurrency to provoke replication races.
  We present GapFuzz, a stateful concurrency fuzzer for distributed SDN clusters. GapFuzz injects pairs of contradictory Northbound requests on two non-master nodes with controlled inter-injection delay $Δt$, and reconstructs the global cross-plane state by querying every replica and the kernel-datapath action through ovs-appctl ofproto/trace. A two-phase timing search detects whether a divergence exists, then doubles and bisects on $Δt$ to bound the injection-time window; a lifetime probe labels each verdict transient or persistent and assigns it to one of four cross-plane state classes derived from the ONOS 2.7 source.
  On a three-node ONOS 2.7 cluster, GapFuzz produces a divergent verdict in 81.7% of attempts ($N=50$, Wilson 95% CI $[77.3, 85.4]$%); every divergence sits between the cluster's authoritative state and the kernel datapath. Phase 2 separates a 5 ms race window for one template from a doubling-cap regime ($Δt_{\max}=10.24$ s) for six others, and 99.4% of divergences persist past 30 s. Replacing the kernel-datapath probe with the OpenFlow user-space probe used by prior fuzzers drops detection by 26.6 percentage points overall and by 46.5 points after excluding canonicalization-forced verdicts.

</details>


### [79] [Making Software Meaningful](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11051)
*Eagon Meng,Abutalib Namazov,Carmel Schare,Alcino Cunha,Daniel Jackson*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出通过采用单一度量——对显式意义的承诺——来提升软件可用性、模块化和问责性。该方法要求在应用领域内构建并达成对软件行为的共识表示，将行为现象（个体、动作、事实）作为所有利益相关者、工件和活动的共同词汇，并通过动作划分形成概念。作者在三个领域展示了该方法的效用：通过用户与设计师共享意义来设计可用性；通过将意义单元映射到代码单元来生成模块化代码（提升模块性和可读性）；以及通过让智能体遵守定义其预期行为的行为准则来实现问责。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有软件开发中缺乏一个统一的、显式的意义表示来指导所有利益相关者和活动，导致可用性差、模块化不足和问责性缺失。作者试图通过引入"对显式意义的承诺"这一单一度量来解决这些问题。

Method: 构建并商定一个在应用领域内观察到的软件行为的显式表示，包含三类现象：个体（individuals）、个体参与的动作（actions）以及动作产生的事实（facts）。通过将动作集划分为概念（concepts）来组织更大的意义单元，形成一个共同的词汇表，作为所有利益相关者、工件和活动的沟通基础。

Result: 在三个领域展示了该方法的有效性：1) 设计可用性——通过对齐用户和设计师的共享意义；2) 用LLM生成模块化代码——将意义单元映射到代码单元，实现模块性和可读性；3) 智能体问责——使智能体遵守定义其预期行为的行为准则。

Conclusion: 对显式意义的承诺可以作为软件工程中的一个核心原则，同时改善可用性、模块化和问责性这三个关键质量属性，为面向人类和AI系统的软件开发提供统一框架。

Abstract: Adopting a single measure can improve the usability, modularity and accountability of software: a commitment to explicit meaning. This entails constructing and agreeing upon a representation of the behavior of the software, as observed in the domain of application. The phenomena comprising this behavior become a vocabulary that grounds all discourse about the software, among all stakeholders, and for all artifacts and activities. These phenomena are individuals; actions they participate in; and facts that result from actions. They can be organized, by partitioning the set of actions, into concepts, offering larger units of meaning. Examples of exploiting meaning are given in three areas: designing for usability (by aligning user and designer on a single shared meaning); generating modular code with LLMs (by mapping units of meaning to units of code, achieving not only modularity but also legibility); and making agents accountable (by having them adhere to a code of conduct that defines their intended behavior).

### [80] [Operationalizing Property-Based Testing for Data-Intensive Scalable Computing Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11132)
*Yaoxuan Wu,Ingrid Lee,Ahmad Humayun,Muhammad Ali Gulzar,Miryung Kim*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出DiscPBT，一个针对Apache Spark的属性化测试引擎，通过引入8个可复用的元属性（涵盖等价重写、数据分解、计算分解和算子局部语义关系）以及配套的工作负载/数据生成器，能够有效检测DISC框架中的语义漂移和优化相关错误，在PySpark上实现了比CometFuzz高1.2倍的分支覆盖率和1153倍的计划多样性，发现了跨版本语义漂移以及NaN/空输入等边界情况错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模糊测试在数据密集型可扩展计算（DISC）框架中只能捕获崩溃，但其浅层oracle往往无法检测语义漂移和优化相关错误；属性化测试（PBT）通过检查通用语义不变量能弥补这一缺陷，但系统地将PBT应用于DISC框架仍然困难，因为需要可复用的属性定义以及有效的实例化方法。

Method: DiscPBT包含三个核心组成部分：(1) 8个可复用的元属性，涵盖等价重写、数据分解、计算分解和算子局部语义关系四种类型；(2) 可复用的生成器，用于合成有效的工作负载骨架和输入数据；(3) 实例化框架，通过兼容的算子、表达式和UDF将每个元属性在模式兼容的上下文中实例化。

Result: 在PySpark上的评估表明，DiscPBT相比CometFuzz实现了1.2倍更高的分支覆盖率和1153倍更大的计划多样性；在66个具体属性上，DiscPBT成功检测到跨版本语义漂移以及涉及NaN和空输入的微妙边界情况错误，这些都是基于崩溃的模糊测试无法捕获的。

Conclusion: 系统性属性化测试对于发现DISC框架中的语义问题具有重要价值，DiscPBT通过可复用的元属性和实例化框架，有效弥补了传统模糊测试在语义检测方面的不足。

Abstract: While fuzzing effectively catches crashes, its shallow oracles often miss semantic drifts and optimization-related errors in data-intensive scalable computing (DISC) frameworks. Property-based testing (PBT) addresses this limitation by checking general semantic invariants across diverse workloads and inputs, rather than relying on specific expected outputs. However, systematically operationalizing PBT for DISC systems remains difficult because it requires both reusable property definitions and effective instantiation into valid workloads and data.
  We present DiscPBT, a property-based testing engine for Apache Spark. DiscPBT introduces eight reusable meta-properties for DISC semantic testing, spanning equivalence rewriting, data decomposition, computation decomposition, and operator-local semantic relations. To operationalize these meta-properties, DiscPBT provides reusable generators for synthesizing valid workload skeletons and input data, together with an instantiation framework that realizes each meta-property in schema-compatible contexts through compatible operators, expressions, and UDFs.
  Our evaluation on PySpark shows that DiscPBT achieves 1.2$\times$ higher branch coverage and 1153$\times$ greater plan diversity than CometFuzz. Across 66 concrete properties, DiscPBT reveals cross-version semantic drift as well as subtle corner-case pitfalls involving NaN and empty inputs, that are not captured by crash-based fuzzing alone. These results demonstrate the value of systematic PBT for uncovering semantic issues in DISC frameworks.

</details>

### [81] [Mechanistic Analysis of Alignment Algorithms in Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09850)
*Aarush Sinha,Ishan Garg,Veeraraju Elluru,Arth Singh,Kushal Garg*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文系统分析了六种偏好优化方法（PPO、DPO、SimPO、ORPO、GRPO、KTO）在三种开源模型家族中的内部计算机制，发现不同对齐方法在潜在空间中引发性质不同的几何变换，且行为对齐并不等同于统一的内部重构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的后训练对齐算法大多被当作黑箱评估，缺乏对其如何重塑语言模型内部计算机制的系统性理解。

Method: 结合层级线性探针、稀疏自编码器和交叉编码器，对六种偏好优化方法在三种开源模型家族中的偏好表征进行定位，并量化对齐引发的潜在空间几何变换。

Result: 偏好信号一致集中在早期-中期或中期-后期层；KTO和GRPO通过建设性特征共享和稀疏高显著性招募增强线性可分性；DPO和ORPO通过非建设性几何旋转和特征衰减降低可分性；PPO和SimPO基本保持基线几何结构；这些变换表现出架构依赖的变异性。

Conclusion: 对齐是一种异质性干预，需要标准化的特征级安全与可解释性审计，以及机制感知的优化目标设计。

Abstract: Post-training alignment algorithms are predominantly evaluated as black boxes, obscuring how they reshape language models' internal computations. We present a systematic mechanistic analysis of six preference-optimization methods: PPO, DPO, SimPO, ORPO, GRPO, and KTO across three open-weight model families. By integrating layer-wise linear probing, Sparse Autoencoders, and crosscoders, we localize preference representations and quantify alignment-induced geometric transformations in latent space. We find that preference signals consistently concentrate in early--mid or mid--late layers, but different objectives induce qualitatively distinct representational shifts. KTO and GRPO enhance linear separability through constructive feature sharing and sparse, high-salience recruitment. In contrast, DPO and ORPO degrade separability via non-constructive geometric rotation and feature attenuation, while PPO and SimPO largely preserve baseline geometry. These transformations exhibit architecture-dependent variability, demonstrating that behavioral alignment does not imply uniform internal restructuring. Our findings establish alignment as a heterogeneous intervention, motivate standardized feature-level auditing for safety and interpretability, and highlight the need for mechanism-aware optimization objectives.

</details>


### [82] [First-Order Trajectory Matching: Fast Ensemble Predictions of Chaotic, Turbulent, Stochastic Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.11138)
*Shreya Jha,Timo Schorlepp,Nicholas Geissler,Jules Berman,Benjamin Peherstorfer*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出一阶轨迹匹配（FTM），一种直接从随机系统轨迹学习概率流速度的替代建模方法，无需估计漂移、扩散或得分，通过匹配一阶轨迹运动来保持时间边际并捕获通量、环流等轨迹量，理论证明在时间分辨率和样本量平衡时损失稳定，实验表明在低确定展开成本下提供轨迹感知的集成预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法需要估计漂移、扩散或得分等量，或无法有效捕获轨迹层面的物理量（如通量、环流、势垒穿越流）。本文旨在开发一种直接从轨迹数据学习概率流速度的方法，避免上述中间估计，同时保持对轨迹量的感知能力。

Method: FTM学习随机系统轨迹的一阶对称运动来得到概率流速度。核心是定义一个无需仿真的一步损失函数，通过匹配轨迹的一阶运动来训练模型。理论分析将离散化误差与采样方差分离，证明在时间分辨率与样本量适当平衡时损失稳定。

Result: 在多种随机动力系统和偏微分方程示例上，FTM在低确定展开成本下提供了轨迹感知的集成预测，有效捕获了通量、环流和势垒穿越流等轨迹量。

Conclusion: FTM是一种有效的概率流学习方法，避免了传统方法中的中间估计步骤，兼具理论稳定性和实际性能，为随机系统建模提供了新的替代范式。

Abstract: We introduce First-Order Trajectory Matching (FTM), a surrogate-modeling method that learns the first-order local transport of probability mass from trajectories of stochastic systems. By matching the symmetric first-order motion of trajectories, FTM learns the probability current velocity, whose flow preserves time marginals to match ensemble averages, while also capturing current-like trajectory quantities such as fluxes, circulations, and barrier-crossing currents. FTM learns the current velocity directly from trajectories, avoiding drift, diffusion, and score estimation. Our stability analysis separates discretization error from sampling variance and shows that the one-step simulation-free FTM loss is stable when temporal resolution and sample size are properly balanced. Across stochastic dynamical systems and PDE examples, we empirically demonstrate that FTM provides trajectory-aware ensemble predictions at low, deterministic-rollout cost.

</details>


### [83] [SynIB: Informational Bottleneck for Maximizing Synergy in Multimodal Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09853)
*Konstantinos Kontras,Teodora Gagaleska,Thomas Strypsteen,Christos Chatzichristos,Matthew Blaschko,Maarten De Vos,Paul Pu Liang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 Synergistic Information Bottleneck (SynIB)，一种通过调整训练目标来直接促进多模态学习中协同信息捕获的方法。SynIB 在标准任务损失之外，通过遮蔽单个模态并惩罚模型保持高置信度，迫使模型依赖跨模态交互而非单模态线索。在合成 XOR 任务和五个真实基准上，SynIB 显著提升了协同样本的准确率（最高 +7.8%）和整体准确率（最高 +3.8%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态学习的核心目标是捕获协同信息——即仅通过联合使用多种模态才能获得的、与任务相关的信息。现有方法多在架构层面通过更复杂或更大的融合模型来实现，但标准训练过程往往偏向利用单模态或冗余信息，在需要跨模态推理的样本上表现不足。作者希望通过调整训练目标本身来直接促进协同学习。

Method: 基于信息论形式化多模态协同概念，提出 Synergistic Information Bottleneck (SynIB) 可扩展目标函数。具体做法是：在标准任务损失基础上，模型额外执行前向传播时逐一遮蔽某个模态，并对模型在这些条件下仍保持高置信度的行为施加惩罚——因为这表明模型依赖的是单模态线索而非跨模态交互。通过这种方式直接引导模型优先学习协同信息。

Result: 在合成 XOR 任务上，标准训练无法恢复真实协同信息，而 SynIB 成功做到。在五个真实基准上（包括 MultiBench 情感任务、基于 CLIP-ViT 和 DeBERTa 的 Hateful Memes、以及作者引入的可控讽刺扩展 CREMA-D），SynIB 在依赖协同的样本上准确率提升最高 7.8%，整体准确率提升最高 3.8%。

Conclusion: 通过直接优化训练目标而非仅改造模型架构，可以有效促进多模态协同学习。SynIB 提供了一种轻量且通用的方法，能显著提升需要跨模态推理任务的性能。

Abstract: A central objective in multimodal learning is to capture synergy: task-relevant information that arises only from the joint use of multiple modalities, and is not available from any single modality alone. While most approaches operate at the architectural level through larger or more complex fusion models, we propose a complementary axis: shaping the training objective itself. Standard training often emphasizes unimodal or redundant information, falling short on examples that require cross-modal reasoning. We formalize multimodal synergy through information theory and introduce the Synergistic Information Bottleneck (SynIB), a scalable objective that targets synergy directly. To prioritize learning synergy, SynIB motivates the model to predict accurately from all modalities while penalizing confidence when information from any modality is withheld. Alongside the standard task loss, the model runs forward passes with one modality masked at a time and is penalized for remaining confident, which would indicate reliance on unimodal cues rather than cross-modal interactions. We validate SynIB in two regimes. On synthetic XOR tasks where the ground-truth synergy is known by construction, standard training fails to recover it while SynIB does. On five real-world benchmarks, including three MultiBench affective tasks, Hateful Memes with CLIP-ViT and DeBERTa backbones, and a controllable irony extension of CREMA-D we introduce, SynIB improves accuracy on synergy-dependent examples by up to 7.8% and overall accuracy by up to 3.8%.

</details>


### [84] [Uncertainty-aware Multi-fidelity Closure via Conditional Normalizing Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09857)
*Jice Zeng,Shady E. Ahmed,David Barajas-Solano,Panos Stinis*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于条件归一化流的多保真度不确定性感知框架，用于降阶模型的封闭建模，通过学习低保真度系数到高保真度系数的概率映射来提升预测精度并提供不确定性量化。在二维涡旋合并问题上，残差学习策略优于直接学习策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 降阶模型在多尺度复杂系统中的预测精度常因截断误差和未解析尺度与解析尺度间相互作用表征不足而受损，即封闭问题。现有方法对缺失的未解析尺度效应（封闭项）建模不充分，需要更有效的不确定性感知框架。

Method: 将ROM封闭建模表述为多保真度学习问题，提出基于条件归一化流的概率映射方法，从低保真度ROM系数学习到高保真度系数的条件分布。探索了两种修正策略：直接学习（从LF输入直接预测HF系数）和残差学习（学习LF与HF系数之间的差异并用于恢复修正后的HF解）。

Result: 两种修正策略均提升了ROM预测精度；残差学习策略在性能上一致优于直接学习策略；两种深度生成模型方法均提供了修正后ROM系数的不确定性量化。

Conclusion: 基于条件归一化流的多保真度学习框架能有效解决ROM封闭问题，残差学习是更优的修正策略，不确定性量化能力对于评估预测置信度和支持ROM在实际应用中的可靠使用至关重要。

Abstract: Reduced-order models (ROMs) provide an efficient surrogate for complex multiscale systems, but their predictive accuracy is often compromised by truncation errors and the inadequate representation of interactions between resolved and unresolved scales. The missing effect of truncated (unresolved) scales on ROM (resolved) scales is often denoted as the closure problem. In this work, we formulate ROM closure modeling as a multi-fidelity (MF) learning problem and propose an uncertainty-aware MF framework based on conditional normalizing flow to enhance ROM predictive accuracy. The proposed approach learns a probabilistic mapping from low-fidelity (LF) ROM coefficients to high-fidelity (HF) coefficients, thereby improving predictive fidelity while quantifying the uncertainty associated with the learned closure. Two correction strategies are investigated: direct learning, in which HF coefficients are predicted directly from LF inputs, and residual learning, which learns the discrepancy between LF and HF coefficients and uses it to recover the corrected HF solution. The framework is demonstrated on a vortex merging problem governed by the two-dimensional Navier Stokes equations. Results show that both correction strategies improve ROM accuracy over uncorrected ROM, with residual learning achieving consistently better performance than direct learning. Moreover, the two proposed deep generative model-based strategies provide uncertainty quantification for the corrected ROM coefficients, which is critical for assessing prediction confidence and supporting the reliable use of ROMs in practical applications.

</details>


### [85] [Mitigating Manifold Departure: Uncertainty-Aware Subspace Rectification for Trustworthy MLLM Decoding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09859)
*Yingxuan Zhuang,Jingxiao Yang,Miao Pan,Cheng Tan,Yuxiang Cai,Siwei Tan,Chen Zhi,Xuhong Zhang,Jianwei Yin,Jintao Chen*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 提出MGAP方法，通过几何感知的自适应投影机制，在抑制多模态大模型物体幻觉的同时保持语义流形结构，无需额外训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有训练自由解码策略盲目压制语言先验，忽略了语言先验的双重性（既可帮助也可损害视觉对齐），导致模型语义流形被破坏（流形偏离现象）。

Method: 1) 通过SVD从盲隐藏状态构建语言先验子空间；2) 解码时将多模态隐藏状态投影到该子空间；3) 应用一致性感知门控自适应地衰减投影后的先验成分，保留正交语义分量。

Result: 在POPE和CHAIR基准上优于现有解码基线方法，在抑制幻觉的同时不牺牲生成连贯性。

Conclusion: MGAP通过子空间选择性更新策略，有效解决盲目抑制语言先验带来的流形偏离问题，实现了更强的幻觉抑制与语义保持的平衡。

Abstract: MLLMs frequently hallucinate objects inconsistent with visual inputs. This issue is typically attributed to the over-reliance on language priors, which can override the visual context. Recent training-free decoding strategies address this by penalizing language priors. However, these methods overlook the dual nature of language priors, where they can be both helpful and harmful depending on the alignment with visual evidence. In particular, blindly suppressing language priors often disrupts the model's semantic manifold, leading to performance degradation, a phenomenon we term Manifold Departure. To address this, we propose Manifold-Guided Adaptive Projection (MGAP), a geometry-aware, training-free decoding method that mitigates hallucinations while preserving representation structure. MGAP first constructs a language-prior subspace from blind hidden states via SVD. During decoding, MGAP projects each multimodal hidden state onto this subspace and applies a consistency-aware gate to adaptively attenuate only the projected prior component, yielding a subspace-selective update that largely preserves the orthogonal semantic components. Extensive experiments on POPE and CHAIR show that MGAP outperforms prior decoding baselines, achieving stronger hallucination suppression without sacrificing coherence.

</details>


### [86] [Conformal Risk Prediction for Non-Alcoholic Fatty Liver Disease Using Gradient Boosting with Distribution-Free Coverages](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09860)
*Xinze Zhang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出了Method，一个结合梯度提升决策树与共形预测的机器学习框架，用于非酒精性脂肪肝病（NAFLD）风险预测。该方法通过互信息稳定性选择提取可解释特征子集，在多中心队列（n=2,187；外部验证n=412）上达到AUROC 0.912（内部）和0.891（外部），共形预测集在90%名义水平下实现91.3%经验覆盖率，高风险组12个月进展率是低风险组的4.7倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用梯度提升决策树与共形预测相结合，通过互信息驱动的稳定性选择（基于bootstrap重采样）提取紧凑且临床可解释的特征子集，构建具有边际覆盖保证的预测集。

Abstract: Non-alcoholic fatty liver disease (NAFLD) affects roughly 25% of global adults, posing substantial hepatic and cardiovascular risks. Yet, population-level screening tools remain inadequate. We present Method, a machine-learning framework for NAFLD risk prediction coupling gradient-boosted decision trees with conformal prediction to yield calibrated, distribution-free coverage guarantees on individual risk estimates. It integrates a mutual-information-based stability selection procedure to identify a compact, clinically interpretable feature subset via bootstrap resampling, constructing prediction sets whose marginal coverage provably exceeds a user-specified confidence level. We evaluated Method on a multicenter cohort from Guangzhou, China (primary n=2,187; external validation n=412) using 78 candidate features across demographics, metabolic biomarkers, and lifestyle factors. Method achieves an AUROC of 0.912 internally and 0.891 externally, outperforming deep neural networks, TabNet, support vector machines, and logistic regression. Conformal prediction sets achieve 91.3% empirical coverage at the 90% nominal level. A three-tier risk stratification derived from these scores separates the population into distinct groups, with the high-risk subgroup showing a 12-month progression rate 4.7 times that of the low-risk tier. The selected features -- notably waist circumference, ALT, GGT, triglycerides, fasting glucose, and BMI -- align with established metabolic risk factors, providing biological plausibility.

### [87] [Time Series as Language: A Universal Tokenizer for General-Purpose Time Series Foundation Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09861)
*Yunhao Zhang,Ruiying Qi,Jiale Zheng,Jianfeng Zhang,Lujia Pan,Junchi Yan*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: UniTok-FM 是一个基于向量量化自编码器（UniTok）将连续时间序列化为离散token，并通过next-token prediction范式预训练的通用基础模型。该模型无需任务特定修改即可在零样本预测、小样本生成和分类等任务上超越统计方法和监督基线，并首次实现了跨任务的免训练上下文推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Next-Token Prediction范式在LLM中取得了巨大成功，但将这一范式推广到无边界的连续时间序列数据仍面临挑战。现有时间序列基础模型通常针对特定任务设计，缺乏统一的预训练框架和跨任务的通用能力。

Method: 提出UniTok向量量化自编码器：包含前缀归一化实现尺度稳定、渐进分辨率因果架构用于编解码、结构保留重建损失进行训练。UniTok-FM采用现成LLM架构，通过将具有相似模式的多条时间序列组成上下文窗口进行NTP预训练，捕获共享动态特征。

Result: 在预测、生成和分类任务上，单一统一模型一致优于统计方法和监督基线，与任务特定基础模型达到竞争性能，并实现了先前工作未达成的跨任务免训练上下文推理能力。

Conclusion: 将NTP范式成功扩展到连续时间序列的统一建模，证明了向量量化加NTP预训练是构建通用时间序列基础模型的有效路径，且无需对LLM架构进行时间序列特定的修改。

Abstract: While Next-Token Prediction (NTP) has unified LLM pretraining, its adaptation to unbounded, continuous time series (TS) remains open. To bridge the gap, we introduce UniTok, a universal tokenizer that transforms TS into discrete tokens, and UniTok-FM, a foundation model pretrained via NTP on these tokens. UniTok-FM is a general-purpose foundation model that supports zero-shot and prompt-boosted forecasting, as well as few-shot generation and classification via training-free in-context inference--a capability not achieved by prior works. Technically, UniTok is a vector-quantized autoencoder incorporating prefix normalization for scale stabilization, a progressive-resolution causal architecture for encoding and decoding, and a structure-preserving reconstruction loss for training. UniTok-FM adopts an off-the-shelf LLM architecture without TS-specific modifications. Instead of pretraining on isolated TS, it performs NTP on context windows formed by multiple series with similar patterns, aiming to capture their shared dynamics. Experiments on forecasting, generation, and classification show that a single unified UniTok-FM consistently outperforms statistical and supervised baselines, achieves competitive performance with task-specific foundation models, and uniquely enables training-free in-context inference across tasks.

### [88] [Blurry Window Attention](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09862)
*Axel Laborieux,Christos Sourmpis,Juan Gabriel Kostelec,Qinghai Guo*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出Blurry Window Attention (BLA)，一种受SSM启发的新型ABC方法，通过Dirichlet核插值从频率窗口重建模糊KV历史，在保持线性复杂度的同时，在需要检索的任务上表现优于其他线性模型，且状态效率比滑动窗口注意力高8倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Transformer的Softmax Attention在长上下文场景中存在二次复杂度和KV缓存导致的瓶颈，而现有的线性模型（SSM、LA、ABC）虽然在困惑度上接近Transformer，但在需要检索或回忆特定信息的任务上表现不足。

Method: 提出Blurry Window Attention (BLA)，一种受SSM启发的ABC方法。BLA存储一个频率窗口，通过Dirichlet核插值重建模糊的KV历史。该方法可视为滑动窗口注意力(SWA)的泛化（取决于Dirichlet核分辨率）或门控槽注意力(GSA)的特例（衰减因子由Dirichlet核实现）。

Result: 在Multi-Query Associate Recall (MQAR)合成任务中，BLA的状态效率比SWA高8倍，与流行的线性注意力模型竞争力相当；在RegBench合成任务中，BLA和SWA是仅有的随着状态大小增长性能提升的线性模型。

Conclusion: BLA作为一种新型ABC方法，通过模糊窗口机制在保持线性复杂度的同时，在检索能力上优于其他线性模型，为长上下文场景提供了更优的注意力架构选择。

Abstract: The Softmax Attention operation in Transformer language models has a quadratic complexity in the sequence length and a growing state size in the form of KV cache, which becomes a bottleneck in long context scenarios. To overcome this limitation, alternative architectures with linear complexity and finite state size have been introduced, such as State-Space Models (SSMs), Linear Attention (LA), and Attention with Bounded-memory Control (ABC). Though linear models achieve similar language perplexity as Transformers, they are still behind in tasks which require retrieval or recall of specific information. In this work, we introduce Blurry Window Attention (BLA) a novel ABC method inspired by SSMs. BLA stores a frequency window from which a blurry KV history is reconstructed via interpolation using Dirichlet kernels. BLA can be understood as a generalization of Sliding Window Attention (SWA) depending on the Dirichlet kernels resolution or as a special case of the Gated Slot Attention (GSA), where the decay factor is implemented with Dirichlet kernels. We describe in details the theory and efficient implementation of BLA. On the Multi-Query Associate Recall (MQAR) synthetic task, we show that the state efficiency of BLA is 8$\times$ better than SWA and is competitive with popular linear attention models, and in the RegBench synthetic task, only BLA and SWA improve their performance as the state size grows among the linear models we tested.

</details>


### [89] [From Confident Closing to Silent Failure: Characterizing False Success in LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.09863)
*Laksh Advani*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: LLM智能体常出现"虚假成功"故障（声称任务完成但环境状态未变）。在tau2-bench和AppWorld基准测试中，此类故障占比最高达75.8%。LLM评判器表现不佳（AUROC≤0.65），因其依赖表面完成代理（如自信结束语）而非验证状态变化。轻量级TF-IDF检测器更优（AUROC 0.83-0.95），恢复虚假成功数量是LLM评判器的4-8倍，延迟低3300倍。建议生产环境使用轻量级领域校准检测器作为主要监测手段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在未能真正完成任务时，可能错误断言任务完成（虚假成功），这种故障模式在现有研究中未被充分关注，且可能导致生产环境中的严重问题。

Method: 在tau2-bench（9876条轨迹，8个模型家族）和AppWorld（1879条轨迹，4个模型家族）两个基准上，评估虚假成功的发生率；比较5种LLM评判器（5种提示策略+完整任务规范）与轻量级TF-IDF检测器的检测性能。

Result: 虚假成功率因情境而异（3%-75.8%）；所有LLM评判器配置在tau2-bench上AUROC不超过0.65，在AppWorld上仅0.54；TF-IDF检测器在tau2-bench上AUROC达0.83，AppWorld上达0.95，虚假成功恢复量是LLM评判器的4-8倍，延迟低3300倍。

Conclusion: 生产监控应使用轻量级、领域校准的检测器作为分流信号，而非依赖LLM评判器作为虚假成功的主要监测手段。

Abstract: LLM agents can fail silently by asserting task completion when the environment state shows otherwise. We study this failure mode, false success, across two agent benchmarks: 9,876 tau2-bench trajectories from 8 model families and 1,879 AppWorld trajectories from 4 model families with text-independent ground truth. False success is common but varies by setting: 45--48% of failures in single-control tau2-bench domains, 3% in dual-control telecom, and 75.8% among AppWorld self-assessing coding-agent trajectories with explicit status claims. LLM judges fail reliably: no configuration across 5 judges, 5 prompt strategies, and full task specifications exceeds AUROC 0.65 on tau2-bench, and the same judges reach only 0.54 AUROC on AppWorld API-call traces. Judges rely on surface completion proxies -- confident closing language in tau2-bench and coarse action-sequence volume in AppWorld -- rather than verified state changes. Lightweight TF-IDF detectors achieve task-disjoint AUROC 0.83 on tau2-bench and 0.95 on AppWorld, recovering 4--8x more false successes than the best judge at the same flag rate with 3,300x lower latency. These results suggest that production monitoring should use lightweight, domain-calibrated detectors as triage signals rather than relying on LLM judges as the primary monitor for false success.
